3285 : HWj 10.1 |HWj 10.1: drak mukṣa ṅ kalaṅön tatan pagalaran ri hayu nira ciniṇḍy (?) anopama. The Utt parallel of AWj has makakalakar, which seems to be connected with determining a number or augury. The bal. com. (KBW IV 750) kĕtekin, kakĕtek, amilaṅi also suggest this. Kĕtek conn. with ModJ pĕṭek? See also carca.  galar I
